  1140	 *  than the server cron.  Frequent short calls provides low latency impact. */
  1141	static long long activeDefragTimeProc(struct aeEventLoop *eventLoop, long long id, void *clientData) {
  1142	    UNUSED(eventLoop);
  1143	    UNUSED(id);
  1144	    UNUSED(clientData);
  1145	
  1146	    // This timer shouldn't be registered unless there's work to do.
  1147	    serverAssert(defrag.current_stage || listLength(defrag.remaining_stages) > 0);
  1148	
  1149	    if (!server.active_defrag_enabled) {
  1150	        // Defrag has been disabled while running
  1151	        endDefragCycle(false);
  1152	        return AE_NOMORE;
  1153	    }
  1154	
  1155	    if (hasActiveChildProcess()) {
  1156	        // If there's a child process, pause the defrag, polling until the child completes.
  1157	        defrag.timeproc_end_time = 0; // prevent starvation recovery
  1158	        return 100;
  1159	    }
  1160	
  1161	    monotime starttime = getMonotonicUs();
  1162	    int dutyCycleUs = computeDefragCycleUs();
  1163	    monotime endtime = starttime + dutyCycleUs;
  1164	    bool haveMoreWork = true;
  1165	
  1166	    mstime_t latency;
  1167	    latencyStartMonitor(latency);
  1168	
  1169	    do {
  1170	        if (!defrag.current_stage) {
  1171	            defrag.current_stage = listNodeValue(listFirst(defrag.remaining_stages));
  1172	            listDelNode(defrag.remaining_stages, listFirst(defrag.remaining_stages));
  1173	            // Initialize the stage with endtime==0
  1174	            doneStatus status = defrag.current_stage->stage_fn(0, defrag.current_stage->target, defrag.current_stage->privdata);
  1175	            serverAssert(status == DEFRAG_NOT_DONE); // Initialization should always return DEFRAG_NOT_DONE
  1176	        }
  1177	
  1178	        doneStatus status = defrag.current_stage->stage_fn(endtime, defrag.current_stage->target, defrag.current_stage->privdata);
  1179	        if (status == DEFRAG_DONE) {
  1180	            zfree(defrag.current_stage);
  1181	            defrag.current_stage = NULL;
  1182	        }
  1183	
  1184	        haveMoreWork = (defrag.current_stage || listLength(defrag.remaining_stages) > 0);
  1185	        /* If we've completed a stage early, and still have a standard time allotment remaining,
  1186	         * we'll start another stage.  This can happen when defrag is running infrequently, and
  1187	         * starvation protection has increased the duty-cycle. */
  1188	    } while (haveMoreWork && getMonotonicUs() <= endtime - server.active_defrag_cycle_us);
  1189

  1191	    latencyAddSampleIfNeeded("active-defrag-cycle", latency);
  1192	    latencyTraceIfNeeded(db, active_defrag_cycle, latency);
  1193	    if (haveMoreWork) {
  1194	        return computeDelayMs(endtime);
  1195	    } else {
  1196	        endDefragCycle(true);
  1197	        return AE_NOMORE; // Ends the timer proc
  1198	    }
  1199	}

  1202	/* During long running scripts, or while loading, there is a periodic function for handling other
  1203	 * actions.  This interface allows defrag to continue running, avoiding a single long defrag step
  1204	 * after the long operation completes. */
  1205	void defragWhileBlocked(void) {
  1206	    // This is called infrequently, while timers are not active.  We might need to start defrag.
  1207	    if (!defragIsRunning()) monitorActiveDefrag();
  1208	
  1209	    if (!defragIsRunning()) return;
  1210	
  1211	    // Save off the timeproc_id.  If we have a normal termination, it will be cleared.
  1212	    long long timeproc_id = defrag.timeproc_id;
  1213	
  1214	    // Simulate a single call of the timer proc
  1215	    long long reschedule_delay = activeDefragTimeProc(NULL, 0, NULL);
  1216	    if (reschedule_delay == AE_NOMORE) {
  1217	        // If it's done, deregister the timer
  1218	        aeDeleteTimeEvent(server.el, timeproc_id);
  1219	    }
  1220	    /* Otherwise, just ignore the reschedule_delay, the timer will pop the next time that the
  1221	     * event loop can process timers again. */
  1222	}
  1223	
  1224	
  1225	static void beginDefragCycle(void) {
  1226	    serverAssert(!defragIsRunning());
  1227	
  1228	    serverAssert(defrag.remaining_stages == NULL);
  1229	    defrag.remaining_stages = listCreate();
  1230	
  1231	    for (int dbid = 0; dbid < server.dbnum; dbid++) {
  1232	        /* Skip the non-existent dbs but not empty dbs since hashtableDefragTables
  1233	         * still defrags the internal allocations of the hashtables structs if they
  1234	         * exist. */
  1235	        if (server.db[dbid] == NULL) continue;
  1236	
  1237	        addDefragStage(defragStageDbKeys, (void *)(uintptr_t)dbid, NULL);
  1238	        addDefragStage(defragStageExpiresKvstore, (void *)(uintptr_t)dbid, NULL);
  1239	        addDefragStage(defragStageKeysWithvolaItemsKvstore, (void *)(uintptr_t)dbid, NULL);
  1240	    }
  1241	
  1242	    static getClientChannelsFnWrapper getClientPubSubChannelsFn = {getClientPubSubChannels};
  1243	    static getClientChannelsFnWrapper getClientPubSubShardChannelsFn = {getClientPubSubShardChannels};
  1244	    addDefragStage(defragStagePubsubKvstore, server.pubsub_channels, &getClientPubSubChannelsFn);
  1245	    addDefragStage(defragStagePubsubKvstore, server.pubsubshard_channels, &getClientPubSubShardChannelsFn);

Now let me create a simple script to test the defrag functionality and verify latency is low:







đźŽ¬ ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_defrag_latency.tcl << 'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env tclsh
# Simple test to verify defrag works and latency is within limits

set ::no_latency 0
set ::verbose 1

# Start a server
exec ./src/valkey-server --port 16379 --daemonize yes --logfile /tmp/defrag_test.log --latency-monitor-threshold 5 --loglevel verbose 2>/dev/null

after 1000

# Connect
set r [redis 127.0.0.1 16379]
$r config set latency-monitor-threshold 5
$r latency reset

# Set up defrag parameters
$r config set active-defrag-threshold-lower 5
$r config set active-defrag-cycle-min 25
$r config set active-defrag-cycle-max 50
$r config set active-defrag-ignore-bytes 100kb
$r config set maxmemory 0
$r config set active-defrag-cycle-us 500

# Add some data
puts "Adding data..."
for {set j 0} {$j < 50000} {incr j} {
    $r set key:$j [string repeat A 500]
    if {$j % 10000 == 0} { puts "  $j" }
}

# Measure fragmentation
puts "Frag ratio: [$r allocator_frag_ratio]"
puts "Frag bytes: [$r allocator_frag_bytes]"

# Delete half to create fragmentation
puts "Deleting half..."
for {set j 0} {$j < 50000} {incr j 2} {
    $r del key:$j
}

after 500

puts "Frag ratio after delete: [$r allocator_frag_ratio]"
puts "Frag bytes after delete: [$r allocator_frag_bytes]"

# Enable defrag
puts "Starting defrag..."
set old_defrag_time [$r total_active_defrag_time]
$r config set activedefrag yes

# Wait for defrag to start
while {[$r total_active_defrag_time] == $old_defrag_time} {
    after 200
    puts "Waiting for defrag to start..."
}

puts "Defrag started, waiting for completion..."

# Wait for defrag to finish
while {[$r active_defrag_running] == 1} {
    after 500
    puts "Defrag running..."
}

$r config set activedefrag no

puts "Defrag finished"
puts "Final frag ratio: [$r allocator_frag_ratio]"

# Check latency
puts "=== Latency History ==="
puts [$r latency latest]
puts [$r latency history active-defrag-cycle]

$r shutdown nosave
exit 0
EOF
echo "Test script created"
